the <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/the-falcon-and-the-winter-soldier-trailer-full/\">first full trailer</a> for <em><strong>The Falcon and the Winter Soldier</strong></em>, one of several big Marvel Studios shows that are being made specifically for the Disney+ streaming service. Now that the whirlwind of Marvel news has quieted down to a whisper, let&#8217;s take a few minutes and take a closer look at the details from this trailer that we all might have missed upon first viewing.<span id=\"more-649824\"></span></p>\n<h2>The Falcon and the Winter Soldier Trailer Breakdown</h2>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-649829 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-1-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-1.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-1-360x154.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>The trailer opens with <strong>Anthony Mackie</strong>&#8216;s Sam Wilson visiting the Washington, DC museum exhibit devoted to Captain America, presumably as a way to remember his friend and former colleague Steve Rogers, who aged out of the position at the end of <em>Avengers: Endgame</em>. &#8220;The legacy of that shield is&#8230;complicated,&#8221; he says to <strong>Sebastian Stan</strong>&#8216;s Bucky Barnes, potentially alluding to the <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/falcon-winter-soldier-isaiah-bradley-black-captain-america/\">in-universe experiments which were performed on Black characters</a> to perfect the super-soldier serum that turned Steve Rogers into Captain America. And speaking of complications: it looks like a different character is wielding Cap&#8217;s shield later in the trailer, so this might be a scene depicting Sam breaking into this exhibition to take the one that&#8217;s on display for himself.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-649832 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-2-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-2.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-2-360x154.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-649834 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-3-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-3.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-3-360x154.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>&#8220;The world is upside down,&#8221; Bucky says gravely. It appears that the two of them are being led through the streets of a Japanese city – perhaps even the same area where Jeremy Renner&#8217;s Hawkeye had that fight in the streets during his &#8220;Ronin&#8221; period of <em>Endgame</em>. (And is that a <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Joss-Whedon-Justice-League-directing-credit-700x300.jpg\">fedora-wearing Joss Whedon</a> that Bucky is about to pass in the screenshot above? Eh, probably not.) Perhaps more importantly: who is that third figure who is leading our heroes into this neon-tinged concrete jungle?</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-649835 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-4-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-4.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-4-360x154.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>Who are these gang members who seem to be behind the shots of explosions and destruction around the world? They&#8217;re grunts who are rumored to work for Flag-Smasher, an anti-patriotic villain who, in the comics, uses terrorism to stoke anti-nationalist sentiment in various countries.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-649837 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-5-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-5.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-5-360x154.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>Sam and Bucky get on Sam&#8217;s family&#8217;s boat (note the yellow &#8220;Wilson Family Seafood&#8221; banner in the background) and open this slick-looking suitcase – which, if I had to guess, might contain the suit and maybe even the protocols for implementing U.S. Agent, a mantle that&#8217;s eventually worn by John Walker (<strong>Wyatt Russell</strong>). &#8220;People need something to get behind,&#8221; Bucky says, implying that the loss of Captain America has left a hole in the nation&#8217;s psyche.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-649840 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-6-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-6.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-6-360x154.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-649843 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-7-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-7.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-7-360x154.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>Their plans will almost certainly be challenged by Baron Zemo (<strong>Daniel Brühl</strong>), the mastermind behind <em>Captain America: Civil War</em> who appears to be paying tribute to his fallen family in this first shot. We <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/marvels-disney-trailer-breakdown-a-closer-look-at-the-falcon-and-the-winter-soldier-wandavision-and-loki/\">already know</a> what&#8217;s happening in that second shot: that metallic hand belongs to Bucky Barnes, who comes face to face with Zemo, points a gun at him, and empties out the bullets. Is there any significance to the fact that only four bullets are removed? We&#8217;ll have to wait and see.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-649846 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-8-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-8.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-8-360x154.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>This is U.S. Agent, who is being honored during a patriotic presentation on a football field. Note that he&#8217;s carrying a shield – perhaps <em>the</em> shield – and since he isn&#8217;t expected to end up being quite the symbol of hope that the world needs, that could be the reason Sam ends up in that museum looking for a shield of his own.</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-649854 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-9-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"Falcon and the Winter Soldier TB 9\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-9.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Falcon-and-the-Winter-Soldier-TB-9-360x154.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>The rest of the trailer contains some pretty solid action beats, including a lengthy sequence following Falcon as he soars through a canyon, dodging missiles from a helicopter. But it all ends with a moment of levity, with Falcon and Winter Soldier engaging in their usual bickering. The question I have is: why are they walking down a random country road? Did their mode of transportation break down? Did something happen to Sam&#8217;s wings? What exactly is the scenario that would result in two Avengers being put in this position?</p>\n<p>We&#8217;ll find out when <em>The Falcon and the Winter Soldier</em> hits Disney+ on <strong>March 19</strong>, <strong>2021</strong>.</p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" &#8220;The Legacy of That Shield is Complicated&#8221;</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com\">/Film</a>.</p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a 6502d17.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/slashfilm?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn26@2020_5/2020/12/12/07-46-09-160_9a442e8760d02cd4.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/slashfilm?i=l03aoI-dh-s:fxH0yGL3eS4:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn14@2020_1/2020/12/12/07-46-10-455_322dfccfa88022d9.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/slashfilm?d=I9og5sOYxJI":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn21@2020_5/2020/12/12/07-46-11-127_879c5505f034c3d2.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/slashfilm?i=l03aoI-dh-s:fxH0yGL3eS4:EGzC5_Ws_ZE":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn21@2020_5/2020/12/12/07-46-10-070_1ad3371a5cd82d3a.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/slashfilm/~4/l03aoI-dh-s":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn91@2020_2/2020/12/12/07-46-08-256_7c5defaa9397c040.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1607759120493},{"createdTime":"2020-12-12 15:45:20","updatedTime":"2020-12-12 15:45:20","title":"‘What If…?’ Trailer Breakdown: A Journey Through Vast New Realities of the Marvel Universe","link":"https://www.slashfilm.com/?p=649798","description":"<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/what-if-trailer-breakdown.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649845\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/what-if-trailer-breakdown-700x321.jpg\" alt=\"what if trailer breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"321\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/what-if-trailer-breakdown-700x321.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/what-if-trailer-breakdown-360x165.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/what-if-trailer-breakdown-768x352.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/what-if-trailer-breakdown.jpg 948w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Disney dropped a new <em><strong>What If&#8230;</strong>?</em> <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/what-if-trailer-new/\">trailer</a> during their huge Investor Day event, bringing us more footage of the animated series. Like the comics that inspired it, <em>What If&#8230;?</em> presents us with alternate realities; versions of the Marvel Cinematic Universe that are either slightly, or vastly different from what we&#8217;ve experienced in the films. It&#8217;s a great idea, and bringing in the MCU actors to voice their animated counterparts makes the whole endeavor even more enjoyable.</p>\n<p>Let&#8217;s dive into the trailer and see what we can decipher.</p>\n<p><span id=\"more-649798\"></span></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.02.54-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649802\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.02.54-AM-700x313.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"313\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.02.54-AM-700x313.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.02.54-AM-360x161.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.02.54-AM-768x343.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.05-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649803\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.05-AM-700x314.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"314\" https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.05-AM-360x161.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.05-AM-768x344.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.16-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649804\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.16-AM-700x311.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"311\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.16-AM-700x311.jpg 700w, 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.30-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649805\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.30-AM-700x307.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"307\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.30-AM-700x307.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.30-AM-360x158.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.30-AM-768x336.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.48-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649806\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.48-AM-700x309.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"309\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.48-AM-700x309.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.48-AM-360x159.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.48-AM-768x339.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Part of the fun of this trailer is that it starts off with shots designed to trick you. Sure, it&#8217;s all animated, but the imagery we&#8217;re seeing is <em>familiar</em>. There&#8217;s Nick Fury (designed to resemble <strong>Samuel L. Jackson</strong>) uncovering Captain America&#8217;s frozen shield, presumably after Cap ended up frozen at the end of <em>The First Avenger</em>. There&#8217;s Doctor Strange&#8217;s Eye of Agamotto. There&#8217;s Star-Lord from <em>Guardians of the Galaxy</em>. There&#8217;s the shot of Tony Stark chowing down on a donut from <em>Iron Man 2</em>. And then&#8230;things change. &#8220;Space. Time. Reality,&#8221; a whispery voice tells us. &#8220;It&#8217;s more than a linear path. &#8220;It&#8217;s a prism of endless possibility.&#8221;</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.58-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649807\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.58-AM-700x310.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"310\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.58-AM-700x310.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.58-AM-360x159.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.03.58-AM-768x340.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The first indication that things are not what they seem comes here – Star-Lord removes his mask, and – shocker! – it&#8217;s not Chris Pratt&#8217;s Peter Quill. Instead, Star-Lord is now T&#8217;Challa, AKA Black Panther! (The late <strong>Chadwick Boseman</strong> reportedly recorded the voice for the character here, although oddly enough, we don&#8217;t hear his voice in this trailer).</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.04.19-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649808\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.04.19-AM-700x312.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"312\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.04.19-AM-700x312.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.04.19-AM-360x160.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.04.19-AM-768x342.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The changes keep on coming. The familiar pod that pipsqueak Steve Rogers entered only to emerge as the buff Captain America opens up to reveal Peggy Carter.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.04.30-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649809\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.04.30-AM-700x313.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"313\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.04.30-AM-700x313.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.04.30-AM-360x161.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.04.30-AM-768x344.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p>And sure enough, instead of Captain America, we now have Peggy as Captain Britain. But Steve Rogers isn&#8217;t entirely out of the equation just yet&#8230;</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.04.47-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649810\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.04.47-AM-700x310.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"310\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.04.47-AM-700x310.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.04.47-AM-360x159.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.04.47-AM-768x340.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.11-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649812\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.11-AM-700x310.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"310\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.11-AM-700x310.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.11-AM-360x159.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.11-AM-768x340.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Meanwhile, in Wakanda, a young T&#8217;Challa ends up abducted by&#8230;Yondu, voiced by <strong>Michael Rooker</strong>. The implication is clear: instead of abducting the young Peter Quill, Yondu took T&#8217;Challa, and that&#8217;s how T&#8217;Challa went down the road to being this alternate-dimension Star-Lord.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.30-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649813\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.30-AM-700x312.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"312\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.30-AM-700x312.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.30-AM-360x160.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.30-AM-768x342.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Remember when I said Steve Rogers wasn&#8217;t out of the equation? Here he is, still in his scrawny form.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-1.29.49-PM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649830\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-1.29.49-PM-700x316.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"316\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-1.29.49-PM-700x316.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-1.29.49-PM-360x163.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-1.29.49-PM-768x347.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p>And here&#8217;s Peggy riding on the back of someone in early Iron Man-type armor. Who is that someone? By all accounts, it&#8217;s Steve. Instead of becoming Captain America in this timeline, he becomes a version of Iron Man&#8230;</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.55-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649815\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.55-AM-700x311.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"311\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.55-AM-700x311.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.55-AM-360x160.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.55-AM-768x341.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p>&#8230;and don&#8217;t worry. These two crazy kids still have the hots for each other.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.44-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649814\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.44-AM-700x313.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"313\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.44-AM-700x313.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.44-AM-360x161.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.44-AM-768x343.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Finally, we meet our narrator. &#8220;I am the Watcher,&#8221; he tells us. &#8220;I am your guide through these vast new realities.&#8221; This character has a name – Uatu, and he&#8217;s voiced by <strong>Jeffrey Wright</strong>. In the original <em>What If&#8230;?</em> comics, the Watcher was kind of like the Crypt Keeper without the puns – he&#8217;d set the story up, and then it would go from there. More Watchers were glimpsed – in live-action form – in <em>Guardians of the Galaxy Vol. 2</em>. In an <a href=\"https://discussingfilm.net/2019/09/06/5806/\">interview</a>, <em>What If&#8230;?</em> series writer <strong>A.C. Bradley</strong> said of the character:</p>\n<blockquote><p>&#8220;He’s above everything else. He&#8217;s above everyone, but there should almost be a gleefulness watching these stories. I keep using this metaphor, which I&#8217;m not too sure if anyone likes, but I always compare it to the pizza rat meme that went around a few years ago. Someone next to the subway recorded this video of a rat dragging a slice of pizza across the platform. I think that&#8217;s what The Watcher is – he&#8217;s a guy watching a rat drag a slice of pizza across the platform.&#8221;</p></blockquote>\n<p>So there you have it: the Watcher is Pizza Rat.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.07-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649816\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.07-AM-700x313.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"313\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.07-AM-700x313.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.07-AM-360x161.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.07-AM-768x344.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p>From here, the trailer goes into the standard &#8220;let&#8217;s throw a bunch of quick shots in your face!&#8221; route that all trailers do these days. The shots themselves are mostly unremarkable – Hawkeye drawing back his bow; Captain Marvel striking a pose; Bucky running around. But I did want to single out this one, which appears to be a <em>very</em> buff version of <strong>Benicio del Toro</strong>&#8216;s Collector character from the <em>Guardians of the Galaxy </em>films. Seriously, look at that chiseled jawline. Dude&#8217;s been working out.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.23-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649817\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.23-AM-700x312.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"312\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.23-AM-700x312.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.23-AM-360x160.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.23-AM-768x342.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The big &#8220;money shot&#8221; comes near the end – although is it really a money shot if it was featured in a previous trailer? Probably not. But here it is anyway – zombie Captain America! This is obviously a storyline that&#8217;s separate from the Peggy Carter storyline, so you&#8217;ll have multiple &#8220;alternative Cap&#8221; tales to look forward to.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.01-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649811\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.01-AM-700x310.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"310\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.01-AM-700x310.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.01-AM-360x159.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.05.01-AM-768x340.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.44-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649818\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.44-AM-700x313.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"313\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.44-AM-700x313.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.44-AM-360x161.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.44-AM-768x343.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.55-AM.jpg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649819\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.55-AM-700x312.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"312\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.55-AM-700x312.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.55-AM-360x160.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Screen-Shot-2020-12-11-at-11.06.55-AM-768x342.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></a></p>\n<p>After the title card, we get a little stinger. All through the trailer, there are various shots of Doctor Strange doing&#8230;stuff. I honestly have no damn idea what he&#8217;s doing, other than waving his hands around and being mystical. But none of it seemed particularly <em>different</em> from what we expect from the character. This final beat finally clues us into what&#8217;s going on here: Doctor Strange ends up fighting&#8230;Doctor Strange. Only this other Doctor Strange has a bunch of red-glowing magic at his disposal, which suggests he&#8217;s <em>evil</em>. How does all of this work? We&#8217;ll have to wait and see.</p>\n<p><em>What If&#8230;?</em> premieres summer <strong>2021</strong> on Disney+.</p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/what-if-trailer-breakdown/\">&#8216;What If&#8230;?&#8217; Trailer Breakdown: A Journey Through Vast New Realities of the Marvel Universe</a> appeared first on <a 15:45:20","updatedTime":"2020-12-12 15:45:20","title":"‘Game of Thrones’ Prequel Series ‘House of the Dragon’ Casts Matt Smith and Olivia Cooke","link":"https://www.slashfilm.com/?p=649886","description":"<p><img class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-649898 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Game-of-Thrones-prequel-series-cast-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"Game of Thrones prequel series cast\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Game-of-Thrones-prequel-series-cast.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Game-of-Thrones-prequel-series-cast-360x154.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p><em><strong>House of the Dragon</strong></em>, HBO&#8217;s much-hyped <em>Game of Thrones</em> prequel show, has just secured three more lead actors.</p>\n<p><strong>Matt Smith</strong> (<em>Doctor Who</em>, <em>The Crown</em>), <strong>Olivia Cooke</strong> (<em>Ready Player One</em>), and <strong>Emma D&#8217;Arcy</strong> (<em>Truth Seekers</em>) are about to take a trip to Westeros to star in a story set 300 years before the events of <em>Game of Thrones</em>. Read on for details about which characters they&#8217;ll be playing.<br />\n<span id=\"more-649886\"></span></p>\n<p>According to <a href=\"https://www.hollywoodreporter.com/live-feed/game-of-thrones-prequel-olivia-cooke-emma-darcy-and-matt-smith-to-star?utm_source=Sailthru&#38;utm_medium=email&#38;utm_campaign=THR%20Breaking%20News&#38;utm_term=hollywoodreporter_breakingnews\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">The Hollywood Reporter</a>, Smith, Cooke, and D&#8217;Arcy have just become the latest <em>Game of Thrones</em> prequel series cast members. Smith, whose credits also include <em>Terminator Genisys</em> and Edgar Wright&#8217;s upcoming <em>Last Night in Soho</em>, will play Prince Daemon Targaryen,<strong> </strong>who is described as the &#8220;younger brother to King Viserys and heir to the throne. A peerless warrior and a dragonrider, Daemon possesses the true blood of the dragon. But it is said that whenever a Targaryen is born, the gods toss a coin in the air.&#8221;</p>\n<p>D&#8217;Arcy (<em>Wanderlust</em>, <em>Hanna</em>) will play Princess Rhaenyra Targaryen, who is &#8220;the king&#8217;s first-born child, she is of pure Valyrian blood, and she is a dragonrider. Many would say that Rhaenyra was born with everything&#8230;but she was not born a man.&#8221;</p>\n<p>Meanwhile, Cooke (who is great in Amazon&#8217;s new <em>Sound of Metal</em>) is playing a member of a different House. She&#8217;ll play Alicent Hightower, who is described by HBO as &#8220;the daughter of Otto Hightower, the Hand of the King, and the most comely woman in the Seven Kingdoms. She was raised in the Red Keep, close to the king and his innermost circle; she possesses both a courtly grace and a keen political acumen.&#8221;</p>\n<p>The report also reveals that <strong>Greg Yaitanes</strong> (<em>Banshee</em>) has come on board the series as a director and co-executive producer. <strong>Clare Kilner</strong> (<em>Snowpiercer</em>) and <strong>Geeta Patel</strong> (<em>The Witcher</em>) have also been hired as directors. They&#8217;ll join <em>Game of Thrones</em> veteran <strong>Miguel Sapochnik</strong> behind the camera; Sapochnik will direct episodes of the series and also serve as co-showrunner alongside <strong>Ryan Condal</strong> (<em>Colony</em>), who co-created this series with <em>A Song of Ice and Fire</em> author <strong>George R.R. Martin</strong>.</p>\n<p><strong>Paddy Considine</strong> (<em>The Outsider</em>, <em>Hot Fuzz</em>) has already been cast in the key role of King Viserys Targaryen, who was &#8220;chosen by the lords of Westeros to succeed the Old King, Jaehaerys Targaryen, at the Great Council at Harrenhal. A warm, kind and decent man, Viserys only wishes to carry forward his grandfather&#8217;s legacy. But good men do not necessarily make for great kings.&#8221;</p>\n<p><em>House of the Dragon</em> is expected to debut on HBO sometime in <strong>2022</strong>. Check out some recent concept art <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/game-of-thrones-spin-off-concept-art/\">here</a>.</p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" Pearson","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Game-of-Thrones-prequel-series-cast-700x300.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn60@2020_4/2020/12/12/07-45-39-800_4782db246bde261a.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/slashfilm?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn26@2020_5/2020/12/12/07-46-09-160_9a442e8760d02cd4.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/slashfilm?i=XrZ1OJpZ3JY:PSWuLH3O-l4:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn87@2020_2/2020/12/12/07-46-07-639_09d1b4a6642b7b10.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/slashfilm?d=I9og5sOYxJI":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn21@2020_5/2020/12/12/07-46-11-127_879c5505f034c3d2.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/slashfilm?i=XrZ1OJpZ3JY:PSWuLH3O-l4:EGzC5_Ws_ZE":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn50@2020_1/2020/12/12/07-46-10-711_54ee5a0eb2045b86.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/slashfilm/~4/XrZ1OJpZ3JY":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn88@2020_5/2020/12/12/07-46-08-232_66780a9959554063.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1607759120498},{"createdTime":"2020-12-12 15:45:20","updatedTime":"2020-12-12 15:45:20","title":"Jamie Bell and Margaret Qualley Are Going to Swing Time Into a Fred Astaire, Ginger Rogers Biopic","link":"https://www.slashfilm.com/?p=649892","description":"<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-649899\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/jamie-bell-margaret-qualley-700x350.jpg\" alt=\"fred and ginger\" width=\"700\" height=\"350\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/jamie-bell-margaret-qualley-700x350.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/jamie-bell-margaret-qualley-360x180.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/jamie-bell-margaret-qualley-768x384.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/jamie-bell-margaret-qualley.jpg 1400w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>You say either and I say <em>either</em>, you say <strong>Fred Astaire</strong> and <strong>Ginger Rogers</strong>, and Amazon Studios says: <strong>Jamie Bell</strong> and <strong>Margaret Qualley</strong><em>.</em> The <em>Rocketman</em> actor and the <em>Once Upon a Time in Hollywood</em> actress have been cast as the iconic dancing duo in a Fred Astaire and Ginger Rogers biopic, titled <em><strong>Fred &#38; Ginger</strong>.</em></p>\n<p><span id=\"more-649892\"></span></p>\n<p><strong>Margaret Qualley</strong> is about to dance backwards, and in heels, with <strong>Jamie Bell</strong> in <em>Fred &#38; Ginger</em>, a new biopic about the cinematic dancing icons Fred Astaire and Ginger Rogers from Amazon Studios and Automatik. <em>Fred &#38; Ginger</em>, which will be directed by <em>The End of the F*cking World</em> creator <strong>Jonathan Entwistle</strong> and penned by <em>A Private War</em> writer Arash Amel, will tell &#8220;the untold, real love story between these two legends both on- and off-screen,&#8221; according to <a href=\"https://www.hollywoodreporter.com/news/jamie-bell-margaret-qualley-to-star-in-fred-astaire-ginger-rogers-biopic\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">The Hollywood Reporter</a>.</p>\n<p>Astaire and Rogers are probably the most famous dancing partners in cinema, starring in a total of 10 films together, including classics like <em>The Gay Divorcee, Top Hat, Swing Time, </em>and <em>Shall We Dance</em>. Not all of those films are all-time greats, nor are the beloved classics imperfect either (each one is basically a rehash of <em>The Gay Divorcee</em>&#8216;s formula, in which Astaire&#8217;s character aggressively pursues Roger&#8217;s character, and they clash only to find a kinship through dance) but damn, did Astair and Rogers look good when they danced together. Their dance chemistry made up for some of the lazier formulas of their films, and resulted in iconic sequences like their <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LOILZ_D3aRg\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">roller-skate duet</a>, &#8220;<a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ILxo-TUkzOQ\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Heaven</a>&#8221; from <em>Top Hat</em>, or my favorite of their&#8217;s, the <em>Swing Time</em> tap dance.</p>\n<p><iframe width=\"740\" height=\"555\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/2QboC9Dldk4?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>\n<p>Bell&#8217;s casting here is no surprise, as the former child star got his breakout role as the ballet-dancing working class boy in <em>Billy Elliot</em>, and he&#8217;s maintained his dance and singing skills in other projects like the FX series <em>Fosse/Verdon </em>and films like <em>Rocketman</em>. Qualley, meanwhile, is more untested, though she managed to hold her own against Brad Pitt in <em>Once Upon a Time in Hollywood</em> (neither singing nor dancing, though). She&#8217;ll get arguably the harder job as Ginger Rogers, having to dance play an icon and dance <a href=\"https://en.wikiquote.org/wiki/Ginger_Rogers\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">backwards and in heels</a>, as the star was famously described as having to do as Astaire&#8217;s screen and dance partner.</p>\n<p>Fred Berger and Brian Kavanaugh-Jones will produce <em>Fred &#38; Ginger</em> for Automatik, along with Bell, Qualley, and Amel. Max Minghella will executive produce under his and Bell’s Blank Tape banner. Gemma Levinson will be overseeing for Automatik.</p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/jamie-bell-margaret-qualley-fred-and-ginger/\">Jamie Bell and Margaret Qualley Are Going to Swing Time Into a Fred Astaire, Ginger Rogers Biopic</a> appeared first on class=\"size-medium wp-image-649753 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-comboshot-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-comboshot-360x154.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>The new <strong><em>WandaVision</em></strong> trailer <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/new-wandavision-trailer/\">released last night</a> gave us our best look yet at the trippy Marvel Studios series coming to Disney+ in January. Clearly something is not right in the world of Wanda Maximoff (<strong>Elizabeth Olsen</strong>), especially since her late lover Vision (<strong>Paul Bettany</strong>) is back from the dead. But that might be the least of Wanda&#8217;s concerns as it appears some kind of outside force is influencing her life. Let&#8217;s see what we can glean from the new footage in our full trailer breakdown.<span id=\"more-649672\"></span></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649746 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-kathrynhahn-blackwhite-700x502.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"502\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-kathrynhahn-blackwhite-700x502.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-kathrynhahn-blackwhite-360x258.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-kathrynhahn-blackwhite-768x551.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-kathrynhahn-blackwhite.jpg 1080w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>The new <em>WandaVision</em> trailer begins in a classic 4:3 television aspect ratio and in black and white, emulating sitcoms from decades ago. Kathryn Hahn questions what a single gal like Wanda Maximoff is doing in such a big house.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649717 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-ringsappear-700x505.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"505\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-ringsappear-700x505.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-ringsappear-360x260.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-ringsappear-768x554.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-ringsappear.jpg 1078w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>But it turns out Wanda isn&#8217;t single, or at least she thinks that she&#8217;s not. She manifests two wedding bands for Vision and herself. It would seem that the evolution of the sitcom and its story will be manufactured by Wanda Maximoff, but it&#8217;s not without elements that allow her to question this reality that she&#8217;s created for herself. How is this possible?</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649718 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-dishes-magic-700x502.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"502\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-dishes-magic-700x502.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-dishes-magic-360x258.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-dishes-magic-768x550.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-dishes-magic.jpg 1073w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>I love the use of classic TV special effects to make the floating towel and glass look as cheesy as the magic effects on shows like <em>Bewitched</em> or<em> I Dream of Jeannie</em>. It frames Wanda in this happy housewife role, but with the added weirdness of her having telekinetic abilities and her husband being an android, even though he doesn&#8217;t always appear that way.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649719 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-bedmagic-700x488.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"488\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-bedmagic-700x488.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-bedmagic-360x251.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-bedmagic-768x535.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-bedmagic.jpg 1075w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p><em>WandaVision</em> plays with the tropes of sitcoms a bit by having Wanda and Vision in separate beds, something that was standard in TV shows depicting married couples in the early days of entertainment. But here she brings together the beds with a little bit of magic.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649720 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-housestatic-700x504.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"504\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-housestatic-700x504.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-housestatic-360x259.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-housestatic-768x553.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-housestatic.jpg 1074w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>However, this happy sitcom life that Wanda has created for herself doesn&#8217;t seem to be completely safe. We see the black and white world warp with color and TV scan lines and static, indicating that this certainly isn&#8217;t the real world.</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-649721 size-medium\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-70s-vacuum-maic-e1607703946520-700x498.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"498\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-70s-vacuum-maic-e1607703946520-700x498.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-70s-vacuum-maic-e1607703946520-360x256.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-70s-vacuum-maic-e1607703946520-768x546.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-70s-vacuum-maic-e1607703946520.jpg 1073w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>An incredible shot inside a glorious 1970s home finds Wanda doing housework by using her abilities to control the vacuum cleaner while she lounges about with a fashion magazine. I wonder if every episode finds Wanda resetting the sitcom she&#8217;s in, starting off as a happy couple with Vision and slowly breaking down as the mental construct begins to crumble around her.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649722 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-house-overhead-80s-700x506.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"506\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-house-overhead-80s-700x506.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-house-overhead-80s-360x260.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-house-overhead-80s-768x555.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-house-overhead-80s.jpg 1073w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>This is just your average establishing shot, but I thought it was interesting that it cut out just before we were really able to see who was coming out of the house. Is it just Wanda and Vision chasing after their dog, or is it somebody else?</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649723 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-crib-butterflymobile-700x501.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"501\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-crib-butterflymobile-700x501.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-crib-butterflymobile-360x258.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-crib-butterflymobile-768x550.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-crib-butterflymobile.jpg 1078w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>Here&#8217;s a teasing shot of at least one of the children that we&#8217;ll see in Wanda and Vision&#8217;s family. Above the crib is a mobile of butterflies, but they suddenly come to life and flutter away. Is that something Wanda is doing, or are these babies already exhibiting powers of their own? We&#8217;ve broached the subject of who these babies are before <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wandavision-trailer-breakdown-arent-they-a-fine-pair/\">in the previous <em>WandaVision</em> trailer breakdown</a>.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649724 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-pregnant-weirdsmile-700x505.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"505\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-pregnant-weirdsmile-700x505.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-pregnant-weirdsmile-360x260.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-pregnant-weirdsmile-768x554.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-pregnant-weirdsmile.jpg 1074w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>Elizabeth Olsen has such an odd smile in this scene where Vision is touching her pregnant belly. That&#8217;s it! Moving on.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649725 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-kathrynhahn-70s-bike-700x512.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"512\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-kathrynhahn-70s-bike-700x512.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-kathrynhahn-70s-bike-360x263.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-kathrynhahn-70s-bike-768x562.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-kathrynhahn-70s-bike.jpg 1073w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>This shot is rather intriguing. Kathryn Hahn&#8217;s character is called Agnes, but many have predicted that she might be <a href=\"https://marvel.fandom.com/wiki/Agatha_Harkness_(Earth-616)\">Agatha Harkness</a>, a witch villain who has come to blows with Wanda in Marvel Comics. It&#8217;s interesting to me that they have her riding a bike through the neighborhood, perhaps as a nod to the Wicked Witch of the West in <em>The Wizard of Oz</em>.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649748 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-vision-70s-house-700x509.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"509\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-vision-70s-house.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-vision-70s-house-360x262.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>Here&#8217;s one of the few shots we get of a human version of Vision in full retro wardrobe as he says hello to a couple of his neighbors. I wonder how it&#8217;s determined when Vision appears as human and not. Perhaps he manufactures this appearance in front of other people only. Then again, maybe it&#8217;s something that gradually breaks down like the rest of this world.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649726 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-katrhrynhahn-70s-700x511.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"511\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-katrhrynhahn-70s-700x511.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-katrhrynhahn-70s-360x263.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-katrhrynhahn-70s-768x561.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-katrhrynhahn-70s.jpg 1075w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>There&#8217;s a new neighbor we haven&#8217;t seen before next to Agnes, and his name is Herb. Is he an outside party caught up in this manufactured sitcom world? Or could he have a more pivotal role like Kathryn Hahn&#8217;s character?</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649727 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-teyonahparris-door-700x506.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"506\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-teyonahparris-door-700x506.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-teyonahparris-door-360x260.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-teyonahparris-door-768x555.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-teyonahparris-door.jpg 1077w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>One character we know will be important is Monica Rambeau, played by Teyonah Parris. This is the adult version of Maria Rambeau&#8217;s young daughter who we met in <em>Captain Marvel</em> and will have a key supporting role in <em>Captain Marvel 2</em>. We saw her get thrown out of Wanda&#8217;s sitcom construct in the previous trailer, indicating that maybe she&#8217;s maybe not supposed to be there.</p>\n<p>Monica&#8217;s presence gets all the more interesting here as she snaps out of her chummy sitcom character role when she realizes that she&#8217;s not sure why she&#8217;s there. We thought maybe she was working with the team of agents who gather around the neighborhood Wanda has seemingly created for herself, but now we&#8217;re not sure. In fact, we&#8217;re not sure if the neighborhood is entirely created by Wanda or if she&#8217;s manipulating a neighborhood that&#8217;s already there.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649729 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-staticdiningtable-700x291.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"291\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-staticdiningtable-700x291.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-staticdiningtable-360x150.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-staticdiningtable-768x319.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-staticdiningtable.jpg 1435w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>I love the build-up of the ominous tone of the series as the mental construct around Wanda begins to fall apart. Here the dining room set phases in and out like television static and scan lines. We&#8217;ve also seen a transition to 16:9 shots instead of the old 4:3 aspect ratio.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649731 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-vision-halloween-700x290.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"290\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-vision-halloween-700x290.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-vision-halloween-360x149.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-vision-halloween-768x318.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-vision-halloween.jpg 1440w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>Things start to look a little more modern with these wider shots, and we see Vision in a Halloween costume styled after his classic comic book appearance. Things are supposed to be weird on Halloween. Something is off.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649730 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-crying-neighbor-700x289.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"289\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-crying-neighbor-700x289.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-crying-neighbor-360x149.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-crying-neighbor-768x317.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-crying-neighbor.jpg 1438w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>There&#8217;s this shot of a woman decorating for Halloween, and Vision notices a single tear rolling down her cheek. Maybe she&#8217;s trapped there. But trapped by who?</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649732 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-clockradio-700x291.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"291\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-clockradio-700x291.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-clockradio-360x150.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-clockradio-768x319.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-clockradio.jpg 1440w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>In one of the few black and white shots seen in the widescreen aspect ratio, Wanda focuses on this radio as a voice can be heard through static saying, &#8220;Wanda, can you hear me? Who is doing this to you?&#8221; That would seem to indicate that maybe this construct hasn&#8217;t been created by Wanda, but maybe it&#8217;s an outside party trying to keep her powers in check.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649733 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-beekeeper-700x291.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"291\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-beekeeper-700x291.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-beekeeper-360x150.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-beekeeper-768x319.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-beekeeper.jpg 1440w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>It just so happens that ominous voice from the radio appears over a shot of this shadowy character, who appears to be dressed as a beekeeper. In the shot just before this, it looks like he&#8217;s wearing a medical mask under the facial net, but in this one, you can&#8217;t make out the darkened facial features. Who is this character?</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649734 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-staticfield-night-shadow-700x290.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"290\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-staticfield-night-shadow-700x290.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-staticfield-night-shadow-360x149.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-staticfield-night-shadow-768x318.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-staticfield-night-shadow.jpg 1440w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>Another mysterious figure appears in the kind of TV distortion we&#8217;ve seen throughout the trailer, perhaps a forcefield that surrounds wherever Wanda finds herself. Who is watching that mysterious figure?</p>\n\n<a href='https://www.slashfilm.com/new-wandavision-trailer-breakdown/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-kathrynhahn-80s-concerned/'><img width=\"360\" href='https://www.slashfilm.com/new-wandavision-trailer-breakdown/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-kathrynhahn-80s-smiling/'><img width=\"360\" height=\"150\" Kathryn Hahn is perhaps a villain in <em>WandaVision</em>, these two shots would seem to indicate that she might be trapped here like everyone else and is being manipulated to be part of this mental projection. Agnes says, &#8220;Are you here to help us?&#8221; as we cut from a worried look to a playful laugh.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649737 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-hummercaravan-700x290.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"290\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-hummercaravan-700x290.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-hummercaravan-360x149.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-hummercaravan-768x318.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-hummercaravan.jpg 1440w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>A caravan of military vehicles are arriving on some rural land. Is this on the way to the  neighborhood where Wanda is living? Are they trying to keep Wanda from losing control of her powers?</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649753 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-comboshot-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-comboshot.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-comboshot-360x154.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>We get the first serious interaction between Wanda and Vision, no longer in the construct of sitcoms. Wanda says, &#8220;This is our home,&#8221; and Vision says, &#8220;Then let&#8217;s fight for it.&#8221; This is one of the sequences that I&#8217;m most curious about. Did Wanda and Vision establish a home together before they were off the grid in <em>Avengers: Infinity War</em>? If this is all some kind of trick and how is this their home? Is this all inside her mind?</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649738 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-flying-sweats-700x289.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"289\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-flying-sweats-700x289.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-flying-sweats-360x149.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-flying-sweats-768x317.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-flying-sweats.jpg 1440w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>Wanda takes off in flight with her hands glowing with the energy she has wielded against enemies in various Marvel Studios movies we&#8217;ve seen before.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649739 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-jimmywoo-agents-700x289.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"289\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-jimmywoo-agents-700x289.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-jimmywoo-agents-360x149.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-jimmywoo-agents-768x317.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-jimmywoo-agents.jpg 1440w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>Randall Park is running alongside some soldiers, reprising his role as Jimmy Woo, who appeared in <em>Ant-Man and the Wasp</em> to oversee Scott Lang while he was on house arrest. Is he involved with whoever may be doing this to Wanda?</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649740 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-staticwave-chopper-700x289.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"289\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-staticwave-chopper-700x289.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-staticwave-chopper-360x149.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-staticwave-chopper-768x317.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-staticwave-chopper.jpg 1440w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>This doesn&#8217;t look good. There&#8217;s a massive force field as Wanda starts noticing the manufactured world around her. Is this Wanda keeping people out? Or is this where Wanda&#8217;s contained environment begins? Perhaps the agents and soldiers have arrived when they pick up on some kind of energy source in the middle of nowhere and this is what they find.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649741 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-darcy-700x290.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"290\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-darcy-700x290.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-darcy-360x149.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-darcy-768x318.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-darcy.jpg 1440w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>Hey, there&#8217;s Kat Dennings as Darcy from the <em>Thor</em> franchise! But she looks pretty damn terrified, possibly looking up at the surge of the force field in the shot above.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649742 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-mindstone-shatter-700x290.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"290\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-mindstone-shatter-700x290.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-mindstone-shatter-360x149.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-mindstone-shatter-768x318.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-mindstone-shatter.jpg 1440w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>The Mind Stone? This was both destroyed by Thanos and then sent back in time after the Avengers retrieved it in their time heist in <em>Avengers: Endgame</em>. Is there a chance that Wanda&#8217;s powers are strong enough that maybe she can manifest another Mind Stone? After all, she&#8217;s one of the most powerful beings in the Marvel Cinematic Universe. <em>WandaVision</em> will show her strength to its full potential, and maybe she&#8217;s able to bring Vision back to life.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649743 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-mindstoneblast-700x290.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"290\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-mindstoneblast-700x290.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-mindstoneblast-360x149.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-mindstoneblast-768x318.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-mindstoneblast.jpg 1440w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>Whatever is happening with the Mind Stone, there&#8217;s a burst of energy that comes from it that blows Wanda back. This is easily the most intriguing part of the trailer, and it will undoubtedly be something that has a big impact on the future of the MCU.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649744 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-vision-window-700x290.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"290\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-vision-window-700x290.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-vision-window-360x149.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-vision-window-768x318.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-wanda-vision-window.jpg 1440w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>In a dramatic, climactic shot, Wanda and Vision stand in their living room looking out the window, a shimmer of distortion outside indicating that Wanda may not have much time left with her husband.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-649745 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-combinedbed-700x290.jpg\" alt=\"WandaVision Trailer Breakdown\" width=\"700\" height=\"290\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-combinedbed-700x290.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-combinedbed-360x149.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-combinedbed-768x318.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/wandavision-trailerbreakdown-combinedbed.jpg 1440w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>But Marvel wants to get one more moment of levity in there by flashing back to the sitcom world, this time in widescreen. The sitcom side of this show is what makes this stand out from the rest of the Marvel Cinematic Universe, and I can&#8217;t wait to not only see how this plays out for Wanda and Vision, but what it means for the rest of the next phase of Marvel Studios stories.</p>\n<p><em>WandaVision</em> starts streaming on Disney+ on <strong>January 15, 2021</strong>.</p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" 15:45:20","updatedTime":"2020-12-12 15:45:20","title":"‘Dune’ Director Denis Villeneuve Slams WB’s HBO Max Decision, AMC Needs $750 Million to Survive 2021","link":"https://www.slashfilm.com/?p=649871","description":"<p><img class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-649877 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Denis-Villeneuve-HBO-Max-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"Denis Villeneuve HBO Max\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Denis-Villeneuve-HBO-Max.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Denis-Villeneuve-HBO-Max-360x154.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>&#8220;Warner Bros. might have just killed the <strong><em>Dune</em></strong> franchise.&#8221;</p>\n<p><strong>Denis Villeneuve</strong>, the filmmaker behind the mega-budgeted movie adaptation of Frank Herbert&#8217;s classic science fiction novel, does not mince words in a new editorial published by <a href=\"https://variety.com/2020/film/news/dune-denis-villeneuve-blasts-warner-bros-1234851270/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Variety</a>. After being blindsided by the news that Warner Bros. is <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/warner-bros-2021/\">releasing its entire 2021 slate of films</a> (including <em>Dune</em>) in theaters and on HBO Max simultaneously, Villeneuve blasted the studio&#8217;s parent company in this new editorial, saying, &#8220;AT&#38;T has hijacked one of the most respectable and important studios in film history.&#8221;</p>\n<p>Read more of his comments below, and get the latest update about what AMC Theatres will need to stay viable through the next year.<span id=\"more-649871\"></span></p>\n<h2>Denis Villeneuve HBO Max Comments</h2>\n<p>&#8220;There is absolutely no love for cinema, nor for the audience here,&#8221; Villeneuve writes of the studio&#8217;s decision, saying that WB&#8217;s &#8220;sudden reversal from being a legacy home for filmmakers to the new era of complete disregard draws a clear line&#8221; and indicates that they are no longer on the same side.</p>\n<p>He acknowledges that streaming services are a &#8220;positive and powerful addition to the movie and TV ecosystems,&#8221; but wants to be clear that there&#8217;s a difference in the type of content that&#8217;s made for the big screen and the type that isn&#8217;t. &#8220;I want the audience to understand that streaming alone can’t sustain the film industry as we knew it before COVID. Streaming can produce great content, but not movies of <em>Dune</em>&#8216;s scope and scale.&#8221; He says <em>Dune</em> is &#8220;by far the best movie [he&#8217;s] ever made,&#8221; and emphasizes how much work went into preparing it for a theatrical release, including the multiple release date delays which were intended to allow the movie to open during a safer time in a post-pandemic world.</p>\n<p>&#8220;I strongly believe the future of cinema will be on the big screen, no matter what any Wall Street dilettante says,&#8221; he writes, ending with a call to action for AT&#38;T: &#8220;So, just as I have both a fiduciary and creative responsibility to fulfill as the filmmaker, I call on AT&#38;T to act swiftly with the same responsibility, respect and regard to protect this vital cultural medium. Economic impact to stakeholders is only one aspect of corporate social responsibility. Finding ways to enhance culture is another.&#8221;</p>\n<p>Sounds like that planned <em>Dune</em> sequel and HBO Max spin-off TV series about the Bene Gesserit may not happen after all.</p>\n<h2>AMC&#8217;s Future Looks Bleak</h2>\n<p>The country&#8217;s biggest theater chain has been hit hard by the pandemic, and in a new filing to the Securities and Exchange Commission, the company lays out its future in pretty dire terms. Despite just raising $100 million, AMC says it needs $750 million to stay viable through 2021 – and even then, it could still face bankruptcy if the public doesn&#8217;t return to theaters in significant numbers throughout next year.</p>\n<p>&#8220;A significant spike in coronavirus cases, together with delays of major movie releases or the direct or simultaneous release of movie titles to the home video or streaming markets in lieu of theatre exhibition, have led to theatre closures, prevented the opening of theatres in major markets and have had, and are expected to continue to have in the future, a material adverse impact on theatre attendance levels and our business,&#8221; the filing stated (via Deadline). &#8220;These challenges have been exacerbated by the announcement by Warner Bros. that its entire studio film slate for 2021 will move to simultaneous release, which may result in other studios adopting a similar strategy.&#8221;</p>\n<p>Things continue to look bleak for theatrical exhibition, and we&#8217;ll have to wait and see if they can hang on long enough for people to return to theaters in droves once a vaccine is widely distributed.</p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/denis-villeneuve-hbo-max-reaction/\">&#8216;Dune&#8217; Director Denis Villeneuve Slams WB&#8217;s HBO Max Decision, AMC Needs $750 Million to Survive 2021</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com\">/Film</a>.</p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a class=\"size-medium wp-image-575697 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/itsalwayssunny-season14-bar-watchingtv-700x338.jpg\" alt=\"It's Always Sunny in Philadelphia Season 14 Trailer\" width=\"700\" height=\"338\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/itsalwayssunny-season14-bar-watchingtv-700x338.jpg 700w,
